04/02/2022, 19:32 - Gb: The Smart India Hackathon 2022 is nearing. I have participated in two hackathons in a row, and I've developed a decent understanding on constructing web-based apps over time.

My improved grasp is due to my involvement with several startups. 

One big concern I saw among first and second-year engineering students was their unwillingness to participate. Many of them had no prior experience building products or participating in hackathons.

My team and I will be doing a 24-hour live stream beginning at 6 a.m. tomorrow. We'll be working on our issue description as well as going through the finer points of many steps to follow while developing solutions.

This endeavor will also benefit me in terms of understanding how real-life applications need attention, and I'm likely to get some feedback from viewers on any errors I commit, making it a win-win scenario for all.

Please engage in the discussion at the link below, leave a comment, and let me know if you'd want me to emphasize anything in particular, and please share it with other students.

Prepare your coffee cups. We'll talk again tomorrow! 

Shubh Jangam, GitCtrl team.

https://youtu.be/sxlFy1NpP50
